<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kreupel.html>kreupel</a> (11491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cruepel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lacking, missing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*krupil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krupilaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Krüppel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cripple</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kribbe.html>kribbe</a> (28116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cribbe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">kribba</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kribbe.html>kribbe</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kribben.html>kribben</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kribbe.html>kribbetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">manger</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">crib</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A simple, unadorned <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">nursery</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">crèche</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A breakwater, usually in a river or other stream.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">very often as <a href = vnd.unilang:krib.html>krib</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">stall</span>, a compartment in a <span class="Latn" lang="en">stable</span>.</li></ol>

***krijgen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a> (234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crigen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*crīgan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krīganą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to receive, to come into possession of (anything ranging from concrete to abstract inputs such as news, gift, punishment, et <a href = vnd.unilang:cetera.html>cetera</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:familie.html>familie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> huwelijkskado <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gekregen.html>gekregen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <b>received</b> a wedding gift from her family.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:idee.html>idee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gekregen.html>gekregen</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopt.html>klopt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know where he <b>got</b> that idea from, but it's absolutely false.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bekomen.html>bekomen</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to be presented with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geprobeerd.html>geprobeerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:televisie.html>televisie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sluiten.html>sluiten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:alleen.html>alleen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sneeuw.html>sneeuw</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I tried to connect up my television, but I only <b>get</b> static.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get, to (manage to) cause to become
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gestart.html>gestart</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I can'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <b>get</b> my car started!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form a passive sentence with a ditransitive verb, with the original indirect object becoming the subject of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a></i>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kreeg.html>kreeg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgereikt.html>uitgereikt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></b> given a prize.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to catch (a disease), to become ill with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkoudheid.html>verkoudheid</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gekregen.html>gekregen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I've <b>caught</b> a cold.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>Krijg</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tering.html>tering</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Literally "Catch tuberculosis", but more similar in force to "fuck you".</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***krim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krim.html>krim</a> (40606)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cream</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">creime, <a href = vnd.unilang:creme.html>creme</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:creme.html>creme</a>, cresme</i>, blend of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">chrisma</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ointment</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">χρῖσμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">khrîsma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unguent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">crāmum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skim</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*crama</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">cramen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scab, skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Breton_language" class="extiw" title="w:Breton language"><a href = vnd.unilang:breton.html>Breton</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="br">crammen</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)krama-</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Irish">Middle Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga">screm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">surface, skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">schram</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">abrasion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kramas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scurf</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="id">krem</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="id"><a href = vnd.unilang:krim.html>krim</a></strong> (<i>plural</i>, <i>first-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">krimku</b>, <i>second-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">krimmu</b>, <i>third-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">krimnya</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cream</span>, the butterfat/milkfat part of milk which rises to the top; this part when separated from the remainder.</li>
<li>crème, lotion</li></ol>

***kroeg.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kroeg.html>kroeg</a> (4976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">krôch</i> or its dialectal variant <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">krûch</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***kronen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kronen.html>kronen</a> (12610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cronen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroon.html>kroon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kronen.html>kronen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to coronate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to crown, adorn with a coronet, wreath etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to acclaim, hail, acknowledge ... a winner, champion etc.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kroning.html>kroning</a> (14023)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kronen.html>kronen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroning.html>kroning</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroningen.html>kroningen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroning.html>kroninkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>coronation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the act or solemnity of crowning</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><b>2010</b>, Gea <a href = vnd.unilang:koren.html>Koren</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> Ratering, John Tamerus, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zwarte.html>Zwarte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koffie.html>Koffie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sterke.html>Sterke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhalen.html>Verhalen</a></i>, Kluwer, page 50:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kroning.html>kroning</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Beatrix <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:recente.html>recente</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschiedenis.html>geschiedenis</a>.
<dl><dd>The <b>coronation</b> of [Queen] Beatrix <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still only very recent history.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Someone's solemn, festive ... installation, acknowledgment etc.</li></ol>

***kroon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kroon.html>kroon</a> (3642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crône</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">corōna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corōna</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruin.html>kruin</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroon.html>kroon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kronen.html>kronen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroontje.html>kroontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>crown
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:regal.html>regal</a> headgear</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> royal power</li>
<li>part of a tooth not covered by gum</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dentistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tooth prosthesis</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> top of a growth</li>
<li>any of various currencies, including the Danish <a href = vnd.unilang:kronen.html>krone</a>, Estonian <a href="English"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroon.html>kroon</a></a>, Swedish krona</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">calyx</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">group of sepals</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">chandelier</span> with more than two arms</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kroonjuwelen.html>kroonjuwelen</a> (35932)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***krop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:krop.html>krop</a> (40604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:krop.html>krop</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kruppaz</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:groep.html>groep</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">crop</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kropf</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krop.html>krop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kroppen.html>kroppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:krop.html>kropje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An unhealthy enlargement of a bird's gullet.</li>
<li>The head (capitulum) of certain plants, especially lettuce.</li>
<li>A tissue growth, a goitre, notably struma.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The throat or rather the whole neck of certain animals, especially <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a>, rarely of humans.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any emotion felt as a lump in throat, e.g. caused by fear, anxiety or grief.</li></ol>

***kruiden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruiden.html>kruiden</a> (7247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cruden</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruid.html>kruid</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruiden.html>kruiden</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>the act of spicing up</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruiden.html>kruiden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to season, to spice
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bekruiden</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***kruik.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kruik.html>kruik</a> (17649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crûke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*krūka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*krogu</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:pot.html>pot</a>, pitcher</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin. Possibly from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> root shared with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">կարաս</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">karas</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pitcher, large jar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κρωσσός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krōssós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pitcher</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Irish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Irish language">Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ga">crog</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">earthen vessel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but the phonetics are problematic.  Also compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">croiccenn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">skin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>. 
</p><p>Cognate with (regional) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kruke</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruik.html>kruik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruiken.html>kruiken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kruik.html>kruikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">crune</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*corūna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">corōna</i>.
